            <a aria-label="NP View: Canadians still stuck in the endless lockdown cycle" class="article-card__link" href="/opinion/np-view-canadians-still-stuck-in-the-endless-lockdown-cycle">
             <h3 class="article-card__headline text-size--extra-large--sm-up" title="NP View: Canadians still stuck in the endless lockdown cycle">
              <span class="article-card__headline-clamp">
               NP View: Canadians still stuck in the endless lockdown cycle
              </span>
             </h3>
             <p class="article-card__excerpt">
              It was one year ago this week, on March 17, 2020, that Ontario implemented its first emergency order and declared that non-essential businesses would be forced to close. A year later, our knowledge of the virus, including how to treat it and curb its spread, has vastly improved, but parts of the province are once again facing another lockdown. Its amazing that, a year into this pandemic, our default response is still to use lockdowns  a blunt instrument that has proven effective in curbing transmission, but which could be avoided if governments had implemented systems to effectively pinpoint and control outbreaks before they spread.
             </p>
            </a>
            <div class="article-card__meta-bottom">
             <span class="article-card__author">
              National Post View
             </span>
             <span class="article-card__time">
              1day ago
             </span>
             <span class="article-card__category">
              <a class="article-card__category-link" href="/category/opinion/">
               <span>
                NP Comment
               </span>
              </a>
             </span>
            </div>
           </div>

             <p class="article-card__excerpt">

Thats about to change, making her glad she waited.
